name:G‚Äçu‚Äçe‚Äçs‚Äçt‚Äç ‚ÄçU‚Äçs‚Äçe‚Äçr
info:Guest Room
info:Stayed in April 2024
info:Solo travelers
info:3 Reviews
rating:5
posted:Posted May 5, 2024
msg:Always wanted to experience Aman Beijing, finally booked a one night stay.  

Upon arrival, Jason at the front desk was very helpful and patient in explaining various items and was pleasantly surprised to hear my room had been upgraded.  

The property and the room are just like the photos but actually physically being there and seeing all the details of the architecture, courtyards, and surrounding nature and birds is like being transported back in time to another era.  In this sense, Aman Beijing accomplishes what no other modern five-star luxury hotel can come close to achieving - making one feel a certain emotion or feeling that they've never felt, or perhaps only experienced in their dreams.  

Everything from the furniture to the layout to the art to the lighting is so tastefully executed and done, the courtyards and grounds are kept immaculate (saw people sweeping away leaves), they even have the older style bicycles available to ride there.

Ate at the Chinese restaurant twice, the environment and lighting is so nice, their dumplings are excellent and also really enjoyed some of their soups and vegetable offerings, very delicious.  

Unfortunately, I was quite sick that day and also had injured my knee the day before.  One of the staff at the front desk noticed my limp and asked if I was okay.  I told her I was fine, just a little sprain.  She went to the back and brought out a traditional Chinese 'Ban Lan Gen' pain relief spray can which she kindly gave to me, saying I could use it and take it with me, very touched.  I think it is moments like these which one will remember many years later.    

All the staff I met there were very kind, during lunch was fortunate enough to meet Ivy, the F&B Manager who was very warm and hospitable.  Then during dinner, after I saw down, a restaurant staff asked if I would like an ice pack for my leg, I asked her if she thought it would help and she replied, "Yes."  They proceeded to bring out a huge ice pack that was able to wrap around my entire knee, providing instant relief.  Finally, when it was time to leave, the very lovely and kind Lucy asked if I would like more ice packs to be sent to my room so I could ice my knee before retiring for the night.  

Even though I was not feeling well, it was an unforgettable experience due in large part to the kind and wonderful staff there.

msg:There are many things to complain about the hotel. Let me first say something positive, because the location is indeed very unique. In such a historically significant place, there is such a quiet environment in a bustling city. It is really blessed by nature. The surrounding trees are all centuries old, and the environment is also very good. I think it is a very good choice to have a good rest here and enjoy the leisure time. Now let's talk about some software issues that really affect the quality of our stay.

I have stayed in many hotels. For example, Capella is the same price. Aman is not just a street away.

On the first day of check-in, I had a suitcase. They sent my suitcase in, and then they didn't care about it. I found that there was no place to put it in the room. I could only put it behind my sofa, which meant that my suitcase was spread out on the ground. First, it would block my way to the bathroom. Second, it could only be placed on the ground, so I squatted on the ground for two days to get things. Well, the same situation, well, it should be equipped with a luggage rack, but they didn't.

I found that my clothes needed to be washed, but I was afraid that the water would be stacked in the cabinet, so there was no place to hang them. I didn't want to hang them in the yard. , I need a place to support myself, preferably where water can drip on the floor. After I reminded them repeatedly, they put a piece of cloth under me when they made the night bed.

I don't know why there are some bugs and flies in the room. I told them, and they said they didn't see any flies. To prove the existence of the flies, I took a photo. I don't understand why there are flies and bugs in such a clean and comfortable place.

Well, the funniest thing is this desk and his chair. When I want to sit on the desk, the chair directly hits the bed, which means I don't put my feet in. Maybe I have to sit sideways to sit in. In addition, the cushion on the chair is also very interesting. Well, it is easy to move. It is actually very inconvenient. After I made this desk, I actually blocked the bed completely. That is to say, if I want to go to bed to rest, my family can only go to the other side of the bed. There is no way. We are poor and can only afford such a big place.

The noodles were all lumpy on the first day of breakfast, but it was much better on the second day, but I ordered a pot of Dahongpao. No one added any hot water for me in the middle, so do I only deserve to drink one pot?

When I was watching a movie, I was very grateful that the movie was shown as if it was arranged for me. But when I left, no one turned on the light for me. I walked out in the dark, and my hat fell in the movie room. Fortunately, they returned it to me in the end. But if you think about it, it is a bit scary to walk out of the movie room alone in the dark. Fortunately, it was not at night, but in the afternoon. On the last day of leaving the hotel, I asked Ctrip‚Äôs butler to help me confirm the time of leaving the hotel on the last day. They told me that they had tried, but the hotel only let me check out at 12:00, so I arranged my next trip according to this time. I never expected that I received a call a few minutes later. They said that the hotel front desk said that they could help me upgrade the process, but I had already arranged other trips. I was just curious why they didn‚Äôt reply directly to Ctrip‚Äôs butler? On the last day of my departure, I needed a plastic bag, so I called the front desk to ask if they had any. The front desk told me that they didn‚Äôt have any. Well, actually, I had no place to put my wet towels and some other wet things. They said they only had paper ones, as if they were very environmentally friendly. When I got to the front desk, the front desk also gave me a plastic bag. I didn‚Äôt understand why it was so hard to ask for a bag?

To be honest, with the same quality, these details management and service really can‚Äôt keep up. The most interesting thing is that there was a cultural class of paper cutting. The teacher saw that I was the only one coming, and I finished it in about 10 minutes. I wanted to talk about the paper cutting culture, but the teacher didn‚Äôt have the patience to talk, and then kept complaining there, saying that after the epidemic, no one asked him to go to class. Maybe it was because the economy was not good, but the question was why? Even if I was alone, they didn‚Äôt have the patience to teach me this culture? Maybe it's because we are in the north, the management is really not meticulous, I think he doesn't deserve the price, I am very grateful that they are trying their best, of course the person in charge will also work hard to implement it, but if you have to find the leader for everything, isn't it very troublesome? msg:The hotel was originally part of the Summer Palace, with an excellent location. Guests staying in the hotel can enter the Summer Palace through an exclusive channel unlimited times. It is especially important to enter the park earlier than other tour groups. Those who understand will understand. The geographical advantage is unique. This is very good.

It has been built for a long time, and some hardware needs maintenance and upgrading. Objective reasons can be understood and accepted. The hotel is currently making improvements in parts.

But as many netizens commented, the hard flaw of Aman Beijing is the software. The flaw is too hard.
The quality of the staff is uneven. It really needs to be improved. Although I was mentally prepared before, I was still surprised.
First of all, the car welcoming master, doorman, and front desk staff at the gate are all very qualified and qualified. I thought it was very good when I first arrived. It was the netizens who were too much.
Later, I was quickly slapped in the face by reality (the eyes of the masses are really sharp).
The service staff in the imperial kitchen (excluding several managers) were extremely inappropriate. I won‚Äôt go into details, but I was surprised when I encountered such a situation in this level of hotel for the first time. It was absolutely not an exaggeration. After the feedback, the manager's attitude and compensation can be felt to be sincere, but it does leave a bad experience.
The big sister of the cultural center has a warm attitude but her behavior seems to have not been systematically trained. There is no standard speech. She chats with employees in front of guests, who is scheduled for the night shift, how many pairs of mandarin ducks are sold, how much is a pair, whether she is tired, etc.
How big is the gap between the staff of the Imperial Kitchen and the Cultural Center and the front desk staff? It is so big that there is already a sense of separation. The staff of these two places makes people feel like they have returned to a state-owned hotel. Are they outsourced employees? . . Why is this happening? The front desk manager keeps cleaning up, and I can feel that she is tired.

The second is the management details. In the afternoon, the Cultural Palace activity was told that it was dough modeling. When I arrived at the Cultural Center, I was told that it was face painting and fan painting. Later, the activity started, and other guests who came over thought it was dough modeling.
The face painting is the kind that children play with in the children's center of the shopping mall. There is no experience and no teaching, and the quality of the brush is shabby. I don't believe that the teacher can draw smooth lines with this kind of pen. The teacher only taught how to paint fans, but he was not proactive. There was no communication throughout the whole process. The elder sister said that the fan was brought by the teacher himself and sold separately. If you buy it, you will bring the painting. Because there is no need for teaching, the elder sister continued to chat with the teacher.
The product introduction page shows that there is a tea room for tea tasting, but it is not actually open. . . And no reason was given. If the hotel focuses on culture, please show sincerity and pay attention to details. The original intention of the policy is good, but the implementation is shattered.

Those who only talk about requirements without talking about price are playing **. The above problems may be ignored in other four-star or even five-star hotels, but this situation should not occur at all when booking Aman for more than 10,000 yuan a night.

I am a local, there is no regional discrimination. I only compare domestically. Our Beijing Yihe and Shanghai Yangyun are three seasons apart in terms of management and personnel. I have always liked this brand. I just hope that Beijing can improve as soon as possible and get better and better.

posted:Posted October 29, 2023
msg:Aman Summer Palace is adjacent to the Royal Garden Summer Palace and was the former dining room, pharmacy, greenhouse and stables. Two-thirds of the entire hotel is an old house from more than 400 years ago, maintaining the layout of the royal courtyard in the Ming and Qing Dynasties. It is full of antiques, carved beams and painted buildings, and graceful. It is worthy of being a representative of luxury hotels in the capital. We temporarily changed our stay to Aman for our wedding anniversary and was impressed by the hotel.
* The hotel upgraded to a courtyard suite for free. Four households share a small independent courtyard, which is very quiet.
* The room is more than 100 square meters, spacious and high-ceilinged, with elegant and exquisite classical furniture. The hotel decorated the room and provided exquisite copper concentric locks.
* Equipped with the Four Treasures of the Study.
* Make a reservation in advance for a private theater (all showing old movies).
* You get sour plum soup when you check in, the dried fruits and Chinese pastries in the room are super delicious, and chocolate snacks are given in the afternoon. Minibar drinks are free, and the mineral water is high-quality ******* glacier.
*Breakfast is available outdoors in the dining room, semi-buffet, eggs Benedict, salmon and shaved noodles, the ravioli are delicious.
* 600 dining vouchers were given, which were used at the Chinese restaurant Aman.
* The reflection of the lake in Jingyingxuan, the weeping willows blowing in the face, the scenery is super beautiful, and the afternoon tea is very impressive.
* The hotel allows early check-in and late check-out, and the hotel is fully occupied for 24 hours.
* Free parking above or below ground.
* Ordinary waiters are dressed in Qing palace attire and will take off their shoes when entering the room. The service is very good.
* Accommodation guests have exclusive access to the Summer Palace and unlimited free visits to the park.

name:G‚Äçu‚Äçe‚Äçs‚Äçt‚Äç ‚ÄçU‚Äçs‚Äçe‚Äçr
info:Guest Room
info:Stayed in June 2023

posted:Posted June 27, 2023
msg:In the summer, I took my baby to visit Beijing, brought the old and the young together, and chose Aman Summer Palace. It was noon when we arrived at Aman Summer Palace, and a delicious pear soup was served as soon as we sat down. When checking in, all the details were explained clearly one by one, and finally I got an exquisite hand-drawn map covering the overall layout of the hotel and the Summer Palace.

The little brother who helped us check in accompanied us all the way to the room, carefully introduced the layout of the hotel, the history and characteristics of the building along the way, and patiently answered our questions one by one, and felt at home.

The long corridor leads to individual courtyards, and soon we arrived at the courtyard house where we lived. With blue bricks, gray tiles and red window frames, tree shadows and green corridors, and traditional key unlocking, there is a simple and quiet scene in front of you.

The green bamboo curtains hang down, and the wooden screens cover it, and the Qing Dynasty-style home outlines an elegant scene. The mud at the bottom of Taihu Lake has been tempered at high temperature and turned into gold bricks alone, glowing in the dark, and the courtyards are not brightly lit, which adds a bit of shade in midsummer.

There are exquisite pastries and fresh fruits on the table, and the seasonal bayberry is quite delicious. There is Lapsang Souchong in the teahouse, and it is just right to soak in a pot with dried fruits.

The mini bar is ready to take, a fresh lemon is in place, and you can mix it with tonic water or soda water.

The bathroom, toilet and washstand are separated on both sides, and the place where the eyes can see is not eye-catching, and the layout has perfect privacy. The spare parts are packed in gourd bottles, which are small and exquisite, and have an elegant fragrance that makes people like it.

The small door to the Summer Palace was one of the reasons why I first chose Aman Summer Palace. From 6:00 am to 7:00 pm, I called the front desk and someone would open it. An ancient copper key seemed to connect time, opening the past and Now. The child has never seen such a key, so the young lady taught him to try it by himself, and the child was very happy to experience it.

The roast duck at the Aman Hall is delicious, and the old Beijing series in the breakfast is quite appetizing. The morning sun shines through the window, as if dining in the lush bamboo forest, which is a quiet and peaceful place.

The 8*25 swimming pool is a perfect size, and the children had a great time.

Ask the brothers and sisters at the front desk for travel information, and you can always get satisfactory answers. Even though there are no answers to questions such as "how to get to Tsinghua University and Peking University", they do their best to help with inquiries, which is really touching.

A good hotel not only has a luxurious positioning, not only has excellent hardware, but also has considerate service and thoughtful arrangements, making people feel comfortable and friendly. All of this has been achieved by Aman Summer Palace.

In some respects, it is not even better than many three- or four-star hotels. Stayed for two nights, entangled again and again whether to check out early.
Let me talk about the good things first, there are two main points: style and location. The hotel is rebuilt from the back kitchen and dining room of Empress Dowager Cixi. It is separated from the Summer Palace by a wall. The architectural style and location of the hotel are unique.
Then there are shortcomings, share some objective problems:
1. Poor sanitary conditions: when you enter the room, you find hair in the bathroom sink and unidentified blood stains on the pillow;
2. Disrepair for a long time: the sewer pipe is aging, every time you take a bath, the water in the bathroom does not have ankles, and the water outside the bathroom is full of golden mountains;
3. Insufficient staff training: The wrong dishes are frequently served for breakfast. In 2 days, 5 different waiters before and after served the wrong dishes 6 times, and they were mostly at a loss after asking;
4. Lack of hygiene/safety awareness: The fruit fell on the floor when the waiter received the dish, and the waiter behind passed by and ignored it. More than ten minutes after the diners left, the floor was still a mess that was not cleaned up in time;
5. The public area is not maintained in time: I entered the movie theater. It has been a period of time since the last screening, but the empty water bottles and popcorn cans of the guests were still left on the sofa before being reminded to clean up.
There are also some hardware problems, such as serious water in the road area outside the hotel on rainy days, water leaks in many public areas, and humid and smoky rooms in the room, so I won‚Äôt comment much.
This time I came to Beijing to check in Yihe Aman specially. I read the comments before I came here, but I was actually a bit nervous and entangled. But because of the Aman plot, it still came. Afraid of the gap, I even made psychological construction ahead of time. But the final experience was still far below expectations.
Bottom line: If it is for Aman's feelings, every Aman hotel is irreplaceable. But if you want to consider comfort, you must think twice before deciding to come.
